class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.95pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王爱弟</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：河北唐山法轮功学员。家住唐山市丰润区白官屯镇田富庄村。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，王爱弟被唐山市丰润区白官屯镇派出所人员抓捕、抄家，被抄走大量私人物品。时隔一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，王爱弟被遵化法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金三千元。现今王爱弟被关押在何处，家属无法知晓。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王爱忠：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1976</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，祖籍中国浙江省金华市，现居住在广州，广东著名民主人士，南方街头运动倡导者之一。王爱忠因长期致力于推动南方街头运动，受到广东警方高度关注。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，六四<span lang="EN-US">25</span>周年前夕，王爱忠被广州警方于家中采取强制措施，随后以「涉嫌寻衅滋事罪」刑事拘留，关押在广州天河看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日取保候审释放。王爱忠是近年来一直坚持发声的民主人士，其在<span lang="EN-US">twitter</span>上的言论一直被中共当局密切监控。此次被抓捕，很可能是因言获罪。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日中午有人打电话给王爱忠，称其车被刮，诱其下楼，将人带走。随后，九名警察到王爱忠家搜查，向王妻出示了搜查证，搜走<span lang="EN-US">29</span>本书，两台电脑，一部手机。随后，还将王妻传唤到派出所，询问王爱忠的交往及言论情况，并警告勿发声。王爱忠随后遭刑事拘留，后遭正式逮捕，关押在广州天河区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日获悉王爱忠案已经移送法院，等待开庭。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王爱忠案将于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日在广州第<span lang="EN-US">31</span>法庭开庭审理。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/202241231.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/202241231.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_86.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_86.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">王宝山：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">河北唐山法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日上午，唐山市公安和国保伙同丰润区国保大队长蔺文军，还有丰润区永济街派出所人员到王宝山工作单位，直接把大法弟子王宝山绑架，抢走家门和汽车门钥匙，在王宝山家没人的情况下，直接非法抄走家中的电脑和七、八台打印机，还有准备给儿子买房子的钱，中午其没修炼的妻子回家，也被绑架到市公安局，下午<span lang="EN-US">5</span>点多，才放其妻回家，将王宝山非法关押到路南区拘留所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，唐山市国保大队伙同丰润区国保大队将王宝山劫持到丰润区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日在没有任何法律依据的情况下，遵化法院以从王宝山家中非法搜查出的打印机、法轮功书籍及真相资料等物品为由，枉法判王宝山五年半，勒索罚金二万元。目前在河北省监狱管理局冀东分局第二监狱继续迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US"> 2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东省江门市法轮功学员。于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被当地<span lang="EN-US">610</span>及警察抓捕抄家，关押在江门看守所。看守所期间，王斌被强迫检查身体，警察用几十斤重的一字形八十公分铁锁把他的双脚分开八十公分，强迫他带着锁上楼梯，致使他双脚流血，身体遭受严重伤害。<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个多月后，日前，家属收到律师发来的江门市蓬江区法院《刑事判决书》，法院竟以王斌用<span lang="EN-US">VIVO</span>牌和中兴牌手机注册微信号建群传播真实消息为由，将他重判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年并罚款人民币三万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">王炳章：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1947</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日出生，河北省石家庄市籍人，基督徒，美国永久居民，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1982</span>年曾在美国创办《中国之春》杂志，被捕前任中国民主正义党发言人、中国民主党海外联合总部顾问；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被不明身份的人在越南绑架后带到中国境内被警方拘捕；<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日以“间谍和组织领导恐怖组织罪”被判无期徒刑。据其家人称，王炳章的身体现在随时有生命危险，狱方已在囚室安放了警报器，要求其一旦感到有任何不适马上按响警报；其深知自己健康状况频危，已经写好遗嘱，希望“请加拿大牧师前往中国为他送葬，并要求做遗体解剖公布死因”。目前在广东省韶关北江监狱（广东省韶关市浈江区梨市镇<span lang="EN-US">7</span>号信箱<span lang="EN-US">6-9</span>，邮编<span lang="EN-US">512140</span>）服刑。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王传煌</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">:</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">周启良、王传煌、汪黎明三人均系江西省武宁县人，法轮功学员，在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年期间，曾因组织、参与制作、印刷法轮功宣传光盘、书刊等行动，学习、传授打印、刻录、装订等技术，使用具有自动拨号及语音功能的手机给他人打电话等，而遭到地方当局严密监控和打击。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，在共同搬运、携带<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年神韵晚会光盘、《明慧周刊》等相关海外法轮功影像杂志资料时，被武宁县警方获悉，当场拘捕，其家分别被抄。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人均被江西省武宁县人民法院一审以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。其三人均表不服，提起上诉，同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，经九江市中级人民法院二审依然驳回起诉，维持原判。目前都被羁押于江西省武宁县看守所。分别刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">王春艳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">黑龙江省哈尔滨市南岗区征仪花园小区法轮功学员<b>。</b><span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被抓捕、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，以“取保候审”名义回家，后又被抓捕，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，哈尔滨铁路法院对王春艳判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，王春艳现被关押在哈尔滨市看守所（鸭子圈）。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/8/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%85%AB%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436585.html#2217234049-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/8/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%85%AB%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436585.html#2217234049-1</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王翠英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东菏泽市牡丹区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生，原中共菏泽市委党校干部，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年退休。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>至<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年度，被评为“全省系统先进工作者”，<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>至<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年度评为“全市系统先进工作者”，并全票通过副处级干部提拔。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日傍晚，王翠英在路边发送法轮功册子时，被跟踪监控的牡丹区公安局警察抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，王翠英被带入法庭，庭审期间，手铐、脚镣一直没有给卸掉。王翠英现在仍被非法关押在菏泽市看守所<span lang="EN-US">.2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月获悉王翠英已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，勒索罚款两万元。家人去找审判长范虹要判决书不给，判决书内容、文号一律不给说，整个过程支支吾吾、闪烁其词，反复询问才得知其实三月十八日已经下达判决书，并说王翠英已提出上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">王登朝：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1974</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日出生，陕西省武功县人，前深圳市公安局罗湖分局三级督警，曾任深圳市保安公司第七公司经理，民主活动人士，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，因在深圳市莲花山公园准备组织一个为纪念孙中山逝世<span lang="EN-US">87</span>周年而做的民主宣传活动，而于<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被拘押；随后又指控他在<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年负责深圳大运会保安工作时，涉嫌虚报保安人数贪污<span lang="EN-US">283</span>万元，被深圳警方正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月底，被深圳市罗湖区法院以“贪污罪”和“妨害公务罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年经二审改判，“妨害公务罪”被取消，贪污数额被减为<span lang="EN-US">80</span>万元，刑期减至为<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年有期徒刑。目前在广东省深圳巿监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王东吉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">于健莉一家七人法轮功案受害人之一。吉林长春市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，四平市公安局、梨树县公安局出动几百警力，包括四平市公安局国保大队、梨树县公安局国保大队、巡警、交警、梨树县辖区内各派出所警察，还调动所辖社区的部份人员，并在长春市当地警察的配合下，在长春市开始了对法轮功学员及其家属的绑架，并到在省内其它地区居住的学员及亲属家中进行绑架。于健莉一家七人在各自的家被公安警察绑架。包括：于健莉、母亲付贵华、丈夫王东吉、公公王克民、婆婆王凤芝、妹夫孟祥岐，及孟祥岐的父亲孟凡军。后一家七人均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其中付贵华和孟祥岐被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其余<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人为<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王凤花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北省任丘市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日在集市上告诉人们如何在瘟疫中自救保平安，被任丘市青塔乡派出所关押两天，家属被勒索钱财二十多万元，于<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日回家，但仍然被构陷，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日从家中被绑架到了任丘市看守所，后被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王凤芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">于健莉一家七人法轮功案受害人之一。吉林长春市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，四平市公安局、梨树县公安局出动几百警力，包括四平市公安局国保大队、梨树县公安局国保大队、巡警、交警、梨树县辖区内各派出所警察，还调动所辖社区的部份人员，并在长春市当地警察的配合下，在长春市开始了对法轮功学员及其家属的绑架，并到在省内其它地区居住的学员及亲属家中进行绑架。于健莉一家七人在各自的家被公安警察绑架。包括：于健莉、母亲付贵华、丈夫王东吉、公公王克民、婆婆王凤芝、妹夫孟祥岐，及孟祥岐的父亲孟凡军。后一家七人均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其中付贵华和孟祥岐被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其余<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人为<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王广学：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省围场县法轮功学员。二零一八年十一月，河北省公安厅指示承德市公安局，对围场县法轮功学员展开侦查，围场县公安受案，与承德市公安组成“<span lang="EN-US">121</span>”专案组（十二月一日成立），对全县法轮功学员监视七个多月，密谋迫害。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，王广学等三十四名法轮功学员正在集体学法，遭承德市及围场县两地公安局警察抓捕。抓捕后的第二天，开始抄家，抄走大量的书籍、设备等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被滦平县法院开庭，王广学被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王国华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川遂宁市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，在成都市新都区某驾校当教练，租住在成都市新都区。王国华因坚信法轮功，曾经遭到两次被关押一年、一次被诬判入狱等迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，王国华正在教练场教学，被突然闯入的新都区桂湖派出所抓捕，随后被抄家，两台手提电脑、两部手机、一台打印机和若干法轮功书籍、数据等私人合法财产被警察劫走，教练车被迫卖掉。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日下午三点半，四川省成都市新都区法院在刑事一庭对法轮功学员王国华视频庭审，对王国华判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">王国廷：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生年月不详，天津市人，原天津市北辰区下辛庄村民，维权者王复春之父，“夏俊峰”式的维权者，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，其所在村庄举行村干部换届选举，有“恶霸村长”之称的黄双来欲求连任，但却遭村民反对；鉴于黄在任期间存在帐目不清、多占土地等严重问题，村民决定推举其子王复春和另一村民衡庆杰竞选村官，随遭到黄双来等人的忌恨、威胁恐吓和打击报复。由于黄双来一直认为其子王复春的参选是受其指使，并唯恐王国廷为人正直，在村中有极高威望，会影响他的村长连任，随心生恶念，于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日带领几名打手（据称皆系黄的亲戚）闯进其家中肆意打闹，其子王复春闻讯前来劝阻并报警，警方却不出警；<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，黄再次指派打手前去暴打王复春，并用枪托将其嘴巴打伤，无奈之下王等人二次报警，警方依然既不出警也不立案；<span lang="EN-US"> 5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，黄第三次带领<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人夜闯其家，对其实施肆意殴打，其子女家人及众多村民纷纷赶往现场，双方发生冲突；尽管王等人立即报警，警方依然消极不作为，结果在正当防卫过程中，致使黄和另两名打手被钝器击伤、死亡；尽管之后其主动自首，但其及其亲友等<span lang="EN-US">10</span>人均被警方抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，经天津市中级法院秘密审判，其被以“故意杀人罪”判处死刑，剥夺政治权利终身；鉴于判决明显与事实不符，其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，天津市高级法院被迫对其进行两次秘审，仍做出宣判：“维持原判死刑，立即执行”；其不服继续上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月王复春与衡庆杰二人死刑复核通过并执行。王国廷重新庭审量刑。后王国廷被改判死缓。目前被羁押于天津市北辰看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王海：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">云南省昭通市人，基督徒，云南省昭通市永善苗族教会神职人员，昭通市昭阳区城区基督教堂牧师，中国在押良心犯。自中共执政以来，一直对基督教等及其信徒进行严厉打击逼迫， 王海虽为官方教会认可的神职人员，曾于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2012</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日在昭通市昭阳区城区基督教堂按立牧职，但依然被云南当局视为需要秘密监控的对象；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">7</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">29</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日，因其恪守基督教正宗教义信仰，拒绝与官方妥协合作，为迫其就范，其父母竟遭恐吓要挟；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月，其被昭通市昭阳区警方莫名带走，自此失联，其父母亦被秘密关押；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日，因其渺无音讯，其妻被迫在微信朋友圈发出求救信息，呼吁外界社会给予关注祈祷；截至目前，其及父母均长期下落不明；据悉，因家中老小均要抚养照顾，其妻正面临极大经济压力，且恐其被人暗杀。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王海乾：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川达州市大竹县法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生，四川省达州市大竹县竹阳镇骨干教师。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共开始迫害法轮功后，王海乾多次被抓捕、关押，长期遭受中共邪党的迫害。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月起，因进京和平请愿、说明法轮功真相，被劳教两年。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，曾被劫入大竹看守所关押，次日被五花大绑，挂牌子，全城游街示众。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，被国保大队警方劫入四川省资阳大堰劳教所劳教两年。屡遭非人道虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，再次与多人被大竹县公安局、达州市“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”等抓捕，关押在大竹县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，被大竹县法院枉判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。上诉到中级法院，被维持原判。现在四川省嘉州监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/12/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E6%95%99%E5%B8%88%E7%8E%8B%E6%B5%B7%E4%B9%BE%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%83%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-%E8%A2%AB%E7%A7%98%E5%AF%86%E5%8A%AB%E5%85%A5%E5%98%89%E5%B7%9E%E7%9B%91%E7%8B%B1-430719.html"><span mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/12/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E6%95%99%E5%B8%88%E7%8E%8B%E6%B5%B7%E4%B9%BE%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%83%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-%E8%A2%AB%E7%A7%98%E5%AF%86%E5%8A%AB%E5%85%A5%E5%98%89%E5%B7%9E%E7%9B%91%E7%8B%B1-430719.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王海芹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省围场县法轮功学员。二零一八年十一月，河北省公安厅指示承德市公安局，对围场县法轮功学员展开侦查，围场县公安受案，与承德市公安组成“<span lang="EN-US">121</span>”专案组（十二月一日成立），对全县法轮功学员监视七个多月，密谋迫害。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，王海芹等三十四名法轮功学员正在集体学法，遭承德市及围场县两地公安局警察抓捕。抓捕后的第二天，开始抄家，抄走大量的书籍、设备等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被滦平县法院开庭，王海芹被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 297.0pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王颢达：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">中国大陆<span lang="EN-US">25</span>岁吉林辽源公民。香港人民的反送中运动实际上得到许多大陆人民的支持，中共当局恐香港事态影响内地，一方面严密封锁消息，删帖删号封群，严密封杀消音；另一方面，对公开表达支持的网民则迅速抓捕，有的被刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">25</span>岁吉林辽源公民王颢达在微博上发布蒙面、独眼，倒拿五星红旗，手持打火机的照片，随后即刻遭辽源警方抓捕刑拘。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">西安市鄠邑区法轮功女学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月出生。法轮功女学员王红、董玉英<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日在鄠邑区将村镇附近讲真相时，被人恶意举报，被将村镇派出所警察抓捕，关押在西安市莲湖区看守所。王红因检查身体不适，被放回家。两人都被构陷到检察院、法院。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月西安市莲湖区法院非法庭审两名法轮功学员，王红坚持自己无罪，为自己做了有理有据的无罪辩护。王红保外就医在家，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日王红被蒋村镇派出所与鄠邑区<span lang="EN-US">610</span>警察在家绑架，现在被非法关押在西安市莲湖区看守所。后王红被西安市莲湖区法院枉判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元，刑期从<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日止。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/27/2021-8-27.html#zip2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/27/2021-8-27.html#zip2</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王洪霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江省嫩江县九三农垦局荣军农场法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月出生。王洪霞、于桂荣<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日发放真相资料，被警察跟踪，于<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日在于桂荣家被嫩江县公安局不法警察绑架，被关押到齐齐哈尔第二女子看守所。（这是王洪霞、于桂荣两人第二次同时遭绑架、构陷，被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，她们两人被绑架，于桂荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，王洪霞当时也被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。）<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，黑龙江省嫩江县法院判处王洪霞<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王红霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日出生，四川省资阳市安岳县人，绰号小莲、小梅、小吴、莲姐，安岳县安岳镇铁峰路<span lang="EN-US">9</span>号居民，前安岳县教师进修学校英语教师，茶叶生意经营者，自由信仰追求者，法轮功信徒，中国在押良心犯。因信仰和长期锻炼、宣传法轮功屡遭四川当局的逼迫打压；<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，曾因锻炼法轮功而被资阳市当局以“利用邪教组织扰乱社会秩序”罪由分别劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半、<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年（三次共计<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年半），劳教期间曾屡遭酷刑折磨；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因外省法轮功友人到成都做茶叶经销考察，当与其会面时被突然出现的成都市便衣警察以“是吸毒犯”为借口强行带走，并先后送到新津洗脑班、二娥湖洗脑班关押；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，被资阳市安岳县警方以涉嫌“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”予以逮捕，并关押于资阳市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，被四川省资阳市简阳县法院以同罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年；其不服提出上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，经四川省资阳市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月；据悉，曾在狱中因绝食抗议而致身体枯瘦如柴，生命垂危；其家属探监权（含约见律师）等遭禁。目前在四川省成都女子监狱六监区服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">王红香</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">：</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁抚顺东洲法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1941</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁高龄。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日上午王红香在东洲区搭连集市，被龙凤派出所抓捕，后抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月家属得知王红香被东洲法院秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，关押在抚顺市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王建：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1950</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，河北遵化市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，遵化多个村镇的数十名法轮功学员几乎同时在凌晨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点多遭到警察的入室抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日王建被遵化市法院宣判<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">,</span></b>被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王建兵</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1983</span>年生，甘肃天水人，独立公益人。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年大学毕业后，便加入北京西部阳光农村发展基金从事农村发展工作，开启长期关注青少年教育及成长的公益职业生涯。曾担任西部阳光基金会农村教育项目主管<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年加入广州恭明社会组织发展中心，作为青少年成长项目和残障社群赋能项目主管及统筹，支持和发起相关社区项目工作。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年起开始关注职业病工人的权益倡导和服务性工作，提供必要的法律支持。王也是国内<span lang="EN-US">MeToo</span>运动中重要的支持者。王建兵原计划<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日送别女权记者黄雪琴经香港赴英国留学。但是，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点<span lang="EN-US">,</span>广州警方于王建兵出租屋中<span lang="EN-US">(</span>位于广州海珠区新港西路<span lang="EN-US">)</span>强行将王建兵和即将出国留学的黄雪琴一同抓走<span lang="EN-US">,</span>并查抄了两人的私人财物。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">,</span>王建兵的朋友于黄埔长洲用于储物的出租屋也遭到警方强行撬锁进入搜查<span lang="EN-US">,</span>并带走大量物品和行李箱。据知情人士透露，目前可以确认两人系被广州警方控制，警方均以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”拘留了王建兵和黄雪琴两人<span lang="EN-US">,</span>并疑对双方采取了“指定居所监视居住”措施。主要原因是涉及日常在王建兵他家中的朋友聚会。警方拒绝告知亲友二人具体下落。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，王建兵家属收到广州市公安局发出的“逮捕通知书”，逮捕公函号为特殊的穗公捕通字<span lang="EN-US">[2021]X2</span>。该通知书显示王建兵已于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被广州市公安局以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权”的名义被执行逮捕，现拘留于广州市第一看守所。黄雪琴家属也拿到了相关通知。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/blog-post_29.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/blog-post_29.html</span></b></a><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_41.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_41.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王建敏</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：山东省烟台地区莱阳市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，山东烟台莱阳市柏林庄卫生院退休医生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日上午，王建敏在莱阳市联通公司大门东侧邮箱投递法轮功信后，被莱阳公安跟踪绑架。傍晚，王建敏被抄家，警察抢走了大量私人物品，包括真相币、真相资料、电脑、打印机等，具体数目不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，王建敏即被关押到烟台市看守所，刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，王建敏被莱阳市公安局非法逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，烟台市中级法院一审判王建敏<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，勒索罚款两万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">王景丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生，黑龙江</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">哈尔滨市双城区人，法轮功学员。在中共<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年对法轮功的迫害过程中，她曾在看守所、劳教所、洗脑班、派出所被关押迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被哈尔滨市道里区公安分局建国派出所抓捕抄家，被关押在哈尔滨市第二看守所；当天哈尔滨南岗区、道里区、道外区、香坊区、松北区、双城区<span lang="EN-US">17</span>名法轮功学员被警察抓捕、抄家、骚扰。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被哈尔滨市道里区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/2022-1-20.html#zip3"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/2022-1-20.html#zip3</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王敬琳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省成都市东华机械厂退休职工、法轮功女学员。王敬琳<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日在家中被派出所警察抓捕，两所住房被警察抄家，大法书籍、真相资料、电脑、现金（约<span lang="EN-US">1000</span>元一元真相币，还有金额不清的美元）等被警察抢走。据悉王敬琳在成都机投镇某小区发真相资料被构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被开庭，当庭未宣，于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日一审判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">.</span>刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王聚才<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南政府信息公开申请人、知名民间维权举报打假人王清同案。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被南阳市卧龙区警方以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，本案被南阳市卧龙区检察院移交至南阳市卧龙区法院进行起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其王清、陈强、王聚才及韩猛<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人被以涉“敲诈勒索案”在南阳市卧龙区法院开庭受审，后王聚才被该法院一审以“敲诈勒索罪”枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，王聚才刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王菊香</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：陕西省宝鸡市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年生，农民，<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被宝鸡市经二路派出所绑架到宝鸡市凌云宾馆（洗脑班），被铐在铁椅子上（除上卫生间外）一天二十四小时不让下来，来例假也不例外；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，宝鸡市金台区法院给下达起诉书及监视居住六个月通知。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被宝鸡市金台区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并罚款<span lang="EN-US">4000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王军平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北石家庄市鹿泉区石井乡栈道村维权人士。因王军平的工人被无缘无故居打成重伤，王军平自<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>起到北京中南海周边上访<span lang="EN-US">13</span>次拘留<span lang="EN-US">5</span>次。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，王军平去镇政府上访，镇长让司机开车离开，王军平到镇长车前要求镇长答复，镇长的司机就殴打王军平。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，王军平在亲戚家被欺骗回家以寻衅磁事刑事拘留，后被起诉。此案<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日在法院开庭，未判决。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王君洲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁康平县法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1976</span>年生，家住辽宁省沈阳市康平县东关乡。在天津市滨海新区生态城当保安。因修炼法轮功曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。王君洲在天津市滨海新区生态城当保安，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日（或<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日）下班时，被滨新区生态城分局警察抓捕，据说是因为在微信中转发香港反送中相关信息。在王君洲被关押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，被天津市滨海新区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王克民：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">于健莉一家七人法轮功案受害人之一。吉林长春市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，四平市公安局、梨树县公安局出动几百警力，包括四平市公安局国保大队、梨树县公安局国保大队、巡警、交警、梨树县辖区内各派出所警察，还调动所辖社区的部份人员，并在长春市当地警察的配合下，在长春市开始了对法轮功学员及其家属的绑架，并到在省内其它地区居住的学员及亲属家中进行绑架。于健莉一家七人在各自的家被公安警察绑架。包括：于健莉、母亲付贵华、丈夫王东吉、公公王克民、婆婆王凤芝、妹夫孟祥岐，及孟祥岐的父亲孟凡军。后一家七人均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其中付贵华和孟祥岐被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，其余<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人为<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">王立芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">王复春的母亲。因竞选村长，原天津下辛庄村恶霸村长黄双来对村民王复春参与竞选恨之入骨，多次带领亲信打手到王复春父母家逼其退选，二老也曾多次报警警方不管。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日夜间<span lang="EN-US">11</span>、<span lang="EN-US">2</span>点钟，黄双来带<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人夜闯王国廷家，暴力威胁王国廷，不准其子王复春参选村长，与闻讯赶来的王复春及众村民发生冲突，黄双来等三人被殴致死。该案<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日一审，天津一中院将“聚众斗殴罪”改为“故意杀人罪”判处王复春、王国廷、村民衡庆杰死刑，王立芳被判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年有期徒刑。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月王复春与衡庆杰死刑通过并执行。王立芳刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王立恒</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">:1979</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出生，山东省淄博市桓台县人，淄博市桓台县果里镇马王村<span lang="EN-US">187</span>号公民；香港占中运动支持者，“恶俗维基”及“支纳维基”二网站骨干成员，“恶俗维基网站恶势力犯罪集团案”受害人之一，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年起，中国大陆及海外有网友开始频繁尝试搭建和运作被称为“恶俗圈”的网络平台，其中“恶俗维基”、“支那维基”和“红岸基金会”三大网站最为知名；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年期间，其因与多人积极合作组建“恶俗维基”、“支那维基”二网站，随深受网站友人好评；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，曾因香港“占中”、要求“真普选”运动遭到中共当局授意下的港府严打，同时中国大陆《人民日报》又连续第<span lang="EN-US">18</span>天刊文批评占中运动，随于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日毅然赴香港金钟占领区，在天桥顶撑伞支持“占中”的学生及市民；但返回后不久，即被淄博市桓台县警方刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，又被山东省桓台县检察院以涉嫌“非法获取公民个人信息罪”予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被淄博市桓台县法院以“侵犯公民个人信息罪”和“非法获取国家秘密罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，因其又重回恶俗维基网站工作，而此时已有多家“恶俗圈”网站频发习近平之女习明泽、姐夫邓家贵的信息（含户籍和照片等个人信息），其所在“恶俗维基”、“支那维基”网站亦将此类信息挂于网上，遂立遭中共当局的打压迫害；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，公安部迅速成立项目组，要求对全国该网站会员实施大抓捕；之后经严格审讯，发觉他们年龄尚小且行为基本无罪，故而各地警方将所抓之人纷纷予以释放，唯广东省茂名市警方想立功，声称要给中共建政<span lang="EN-US">70</span>周年献大礼，遂移花接木嫁祸“恶俗维基”，把该警局所属的网站会员（含其在内）尽都抓捕，并上报公安部谎称“破获了一起与反华势力相勾结的恶势力集团大案”；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其被广东省茂名市警方跨省抓捕，并被指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，又被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”等转刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被茂名市检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪、侵犯公民个人信息罪”予以批捕；据悉曾因资料不足，而被检察院几次退侦和被地方法院数次退回要求重新起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">24</span>人“涉恶势力犯罪集团案”被广东省茂名市茂南区法院开庭受审；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其案<span lang="EN-US">24</span>人均被宣判，王立恒被该法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”（判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年），“侵犯公民个人信息罪”（判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月），二罪并罚，决定执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日；其等均表不服，已经上诉；二审维持原判。目前王立恒被羁押于佛山市南海区看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王利芹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，云南省昆明市人，又名王丽，职业不详，著名自由派先锋诗人及作家王藏（本名王玉文）之妻，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。自从与自由派先锋诗人、作家王藏结婚以来，虽低调生活，但仍因其夫是异见诗人屡遭北京、昆明等地当局牵连与恐吓；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，曾因其夫王藏被云南省楚雄市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”拘捕，而遭当局指使的不明人士抢劫，且被以若拒绝与警方合作，家即被逼迁和断水断电，甚至“会弄死孩子”等做要挟，致其因恐惧伤及<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个幼子而得精神分裂症；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，曾因云南当局强行要求王藏一家从北京迁回云南昆明原籍，其又被不明人士威胁、殴打，故而精神再度失常，导致其抑郁症发作，严重时曾出现精神恍惚、昏迷不醒，离家出走甚至跳湖自杀等现象；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其夫王藏被云南省楚雄市警方突然以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”带走刑拘，自此失联，因其夫多日毫无下落，其被迫无奈，遂在各路网站（尤其是<span lang="EN-US">twitter</span>）携子为丈夫被抓捕呼吁，以求正义人士广泛关注与声援，后得知其夫已于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被云南省楚雄州检察院以同罪名正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，因其在<span lang="EN-US">twitter</span>上为丈夫呼吁受株连，亦被楚雄州检察院以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”批捕；据悉，其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个幼子被长期囚禁家中，除准予姥姥临时照看外，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>幼子已多日未见父母；友人恐其因此而使抑郁症倾向加重。目前被羁押于楚雄州看守所（云南省楚雄市鹿城镇福塔小区上平山村，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">675000</span>）。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，王藏（王玉文）、王利芹夫妇涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权案遭延期审限，本案最后审限从<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日再延期<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_86.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_86.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王丽志：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">大连市金州区石河镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日晚，谷秀华（女）、刘希永（男）、周兴（男）、李天学（男）、王丽志（女）、张三曼（女）、谭春荣（女）、孙宝英（女）、刘井龙（男），去大连市金普新区炮台镇袁屯村发放新书《共产主义的终极目的》，被炮台镇派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日下午二在大连市金州法院庭审。后谷秀华、周兴、王丽志，被大连市金州法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；张三曼、谭春荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，李天学被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，刘希永、孙宝英、刘井龙的情况还不清楚。王丽志刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王琳琳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">网名‘我在红尘你在天上<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>’。女，安徽人士，徽乡网总监，因于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日<span lang="EN-US">15</span>时通过新浪微博发布消息称：安徽颖上夏桥镇拆迁逼死老人，发微博的同时附有一段十秒钟显示，视频中显示有多名身着“特警”字样服装的彪形大汉，队形整齐，臂戴红色袖套，蒙着黑色头套，到一处疑似办丧事的地方“执法”。该视频早前已被微博官方删除。后王琳琳于在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日晚被以涉嫌“敲诈勒索未遂”罪抓捕关押，后王琳琳因揭发熊德超领导下的颍上拆迁逼死老人、美好乡村虚假惠民工程，而被重判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。此案正在申诉中。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王楣泓<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省牡丹江市法轮功学员，牡丹江市地质勘察所高级工程师，丈夫于宗海是画家，就职于牡丹江市图书馆。夫妻俩因修炼法轮功曾被判十多年。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，王楣泓被牡丹江市爱民区中级法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，被关押到黑龙江省女子监狱迫害，曾多次遭酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年获释。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日又被哈尔滨市南岗区公安分局哈西派出所警察抓捕构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被哈尔滨市道里区法院庭审。后获悉，王楣泓被哈尔滨市道里区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月初投入黑龙江女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日在昆明官渡区牛街庄圣马网吧旁被公安抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>华检察院出庭指控：王美玲在网吧路旁散发法轮功真相材料，在包中有<span lang="EN-US">1</span>些法轮功资料，及在楚雄的住所有法轮功材料及光盘，并称在案件侦查过程中王美玲大肆宣传法轮功，曾经被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日上午，王美玲被<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">王美卿：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">湖北省荆州市荆州区法轮功学员。荆州市荆州区法轮功学员王美卿、刘新安、仇运凤、邓永梅<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日晚上，开着汽车在马山（荆州与当阳、枝江交界处）发放法轮功资料时、被人举报，被当阳市（属湖北宜昌市管辖）草埠湖派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日当阳市法院下达了判决书：仇运凤被判处<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/10/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436647.html#2219223842-2"><b minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王梅英</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：湖南省衡阳市衡山县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份王梅英在广州大学城发法轮功资料，被监控器监视到。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，王梅英被衡山县公安局伙同广州市番禺区分局警察从衡山县社保局家中抓捕，关押在广州市番禺沙湾看守所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日王梅英被广州市海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。信息来源：</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/29/%E6%B9%96%E5%8D%97%E8%A1%A1%E5%B1%B1%E5%8E%BF%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E7%8E%8B%E6%A2%85%E8%8B%B1%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-434165.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/29/%E6%B9%96%E5%8D%97%E8%A1%A1%E5%B1%B1%E5%8E%BF%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E7%8E%8B%E6%A2%85%E8%8B%B1%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-434165.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王明海：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽省人，基督徒，安徽省芜湖市基督教某家庭教会事工人员，教会学校老师，中国在押良心犯。因信仰基督，并在安徽省芜湖市基督教某家庭教会的教育学堂事工当老师，遂遭中共安徽当局在意识形态方面的严厉打压；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，突遭冲击，被芜湖市戈江区警方闯入教学点，将包括其在内的十名老师悉数带走，教学点亦遭查抄，内中一切物品均被扣押，后其十人被视为同案犯，统一被芜湖市戈江区警方以涉嫌“非法经营罪”拘押；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初，除杨志言等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>名老师被取保候审外，王明海及万红霞等另<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名老师均被芜湖市戈江区检察院以同罪由正式批捕；据悉，其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人案已有律师代理。目前被羁押于芜湖市第一看守所（安徽省芜湖市戈江区火龙岗镇白马山村，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">241000</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王明全：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">甘肃省庆阳市环县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年出生，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年开始修炼法轮功，身心受益。王明全<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被环县环城派出所警察从家中抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，王明全被环县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王默：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刚刚获释一个多月的政治犯王默<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日再遭刑事拘留，具体原因还不清楚。王默曾被判刑有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日才刑满释放。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王默<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年出生，江苏省淮安市人，网名“菜刀王默”，人称“黑犬”，民间知名新浪微博“转世党”，南方街头运动践行者。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，因在广州市多地拉横幅声援香港民主抗争、“真普选”，被警方从广州市增城区新塘镇带走，并被以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被广州市检察院更换罪名，以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式批捕，并被羁押于广州市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日其案在广州中院开庭受理，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被广州市中级法院一审判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。后在广东省韶关市乐昌监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。获释一个月后，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，又被江苏省淮安市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，先被羁押于江苏省淮安市看守所。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月有维权朋友去探访王默父亲，获悉王默已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，现在关押到江苏省南京监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">王朋影：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，吉林省舒兰市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年近七十岁。在中共对法轮功的迫害中，王朋影多次被绑架，曾三次被劳教，一次被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，王朋影出门办事，被警察抓捕，关押在吉林市看守所迫害。后获悉，王朋影被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王鹏义：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省抚顺市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1949</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">72</span>岁王。王鹏义是军队转业干部，在军队为国家服务多年，转业到抚顺市粮食局所属企业。在中共江泽民集团发动的对法轮功的迫害<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多年中，王鹏义遭受了多次抓捕、劳教、判刑，受到多种酷刑折磨，九死一生，身心受到极大的伤害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，王鹏义失踪，经常与他在一起的亲友也联系不上他。一年半以后获悉，他又被抚顺市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现在在沈阳沈北新区康家山监狱二监区。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/22/2021-12-22.html#zip4"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/22/2021-12-22.html#zip4</span></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王齐花：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年六十六岁，家住武汉市新洲区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日上午十点多钟，村部会计何胜伢带领新洲区国保大队四人和旧街派出所一人，闯入王齐花家中，非法抄家，其中一人带着摄像机在家里到处摄像，来人看到王齐花家里挂的匾额十字绣艺术品（绣有法轮大法好和莲花），就强行摘下带走，还搜出几部旧手机，这群人就走了。后被新洲区国保大队和当地警察绑架到蔡甸区玉笋山洗脑班，几天后关到第一女子看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，武汉新洲区法院判王齐花八年有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王芹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东聊城市东昌府区名法轮功学员。张淑萍、王芹<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被聊城市东昌府区<span lang="EN-US">610</span>、国保大队、柳园派出所警察等抄家。王芹被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月左右被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/25/2021-9-25.html#zip1"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/25/2021-9-25.html#zip1</span></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王清：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1982</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日出生<span lang="EN-US">,</span>河南省南阳市人，政府信息公开申请人，知名民间维权举报打假人，中国在押维权人士。十多年前，曾因向河南省南阳市“<span lang="EN-US">181</span>个政府部门申请信息公开”，引起社会热议，但被官方视为“河南刁民”；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，又曾因举报打假而被网络评选为“<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年十大公民”之一，自此其维权行为更是全国闻名；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，曾因将有官方支持背景，且有违法经营操作的南阳市逸美时光咖啡店投诉到当地工商管理部门，期间虽经两次调解未果，但在其不懈努力下，最终迫使工商机关依法对该店做出罚款<span lang="EN-US">45000</span>元措施，并于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年向当地法院提出予以强制执行申请；然而其正义维权行为却因触碰了当地权贵集团的利益，遂遭官商勾结势力的打击报复；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被南阳市卧龙区警方以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”刑拘，后被卧龙区检察院快速批捕，并被指控，因其在向各级工商管理部门进行投诉举报时有“威胁恐吓敲诈勒索商家”之嫌，故而触犯了政府相关法律；另有陈强、王聚才及韩猛等三名维权打假者亦作为同案犯被相继逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，其案被南阳市卧龙区检察院移交至南阳市卧龙区法院进行起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人涉“敲诈勒索案”在南阳市卧龙区法院开庭受审，后被该法院一审以“敲诈勒索罪”枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，另三人亦被分别枉判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年不等，并处罚金若干；其不服判决，立即提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，经南阳市中级法院二审裁决：驳回上诉，维持原判，目前被羁押于南阳市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王庆<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 11.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖北孝感市汉川市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，肖艳芳、刘义波、王四美、王庆、舒运兰等<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人到汉川市马鞍乡联洪村、天成村告诉村民法轮功遭迫害真相及避疫良方，被村民举报，遭马鞍派出所警察抓捕。第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人因疫情原因被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，汉川市公安局对肖艳芳、刘义波、王庆、王四美、舒运兰<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人下达「监视居住通知书」。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日肖艳芳、刘义波被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，汉川国保人员到湖南长沙，将流落在外打工的法轮功学员王庆抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，汉川市公安局分水派出所警察在分水镇抓捕了王四美和另一名法轮功学员胡汉姣。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月下旬，孝昌县法院作出判决，胡汉姣、王四美遭判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刘义波遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，肖艳芳遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，王庆遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。胡汉姣刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王庆英</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：女，河南省济源市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生，任召军的母亲。河南省济源市轵城镇西留养村人。河南省济源市法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1988</span>年生，河南省济源市轵城镇西留养村人。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，济源市公安局“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”警察李建锋带领多人使用梯子翻墙跳入任召军家的院内后，又破门闯入任召军的房内，翻箱倒柜，抄走了电脑、打印机、手机、银行卡、银行存折、大法书籍以及其它部份财物等<span lang="EN-US">34</span>件，又绑抓捕了任召军及父母一家三人到济源市看守所。一个月后，父亲任宗禄被“取保候审”回家。任召军和王庆英被济源市检察院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年十<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，济源市法院宣布判任召军<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年刑期并且罚款二万五千元，判王庆英<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月刑期并且罚款六千元。随后，任召军和母亲王庆英均上诉到济源市中级法院，但均被驳回，维持非法原判。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，王庆英被遣送到河南省女子监狱，任召军仍然被非法关押在河南省济源市看守所。王庆英刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王秋萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">沈阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生。因修炼法轮功，王秋萍曾经被关押在马三家劳教所迫害<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多。王秋萍于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日因发放疫情周刊被一位武警恶告。送到马路湾派出所，搜走了随身带的<span lang="EN-US">1</span>千多元钱和手表、自行车和<span lang="EN-US">1</span>张封城期间的某小区通行证。由两个和平区国保大队的人连打带骂的审问，王秋萍不配合迫害，没报名，没签字，半夜逃走。王秋萍于<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，再次被抓捕，送往和平区精神病院迫害。王秋萍被关押在精神病院<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个半月多后，于<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被和平区国保大队、马路湾派出所警察送往沈阳市第二看守所迫害。看守所拒绝家人送衣物、存钱，更不许律师接见。王秋萍<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，被关押到辽宁省女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: lang="EN-US">28</span>日上午被刑事拘留，被抓捕的理由竟然是“偷越边境”。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，山西汾阳张立功、张耀文、王润云、王世强、宋守山等五位基督徒“偷越国境”一案开庭，未宣判。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，山西汾阳张立功、王润云、王世强、张耀文、宋守山等五位基督徒因涉嫌“偷越国境罪”案一审宣判，分别是被判：<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月（两人）、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月（两人）。判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月的将于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出狱，然后是<span
