lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，温雨飞向齐齐哈尔市昂昂溪区检察院递交了<span lang="EN-US">1</span>份对齐齐哈尔市昂昂溪区国保大队违法行为的控告书。温雨飞向检察院递交控告书后，齐齐哈尔市昂昂溪区公安分局国保大队实施报复。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，派出所以让温雨飞去市检察院说明情况为借口，把温雨飞劫往齐齐哈尔市检察院，返回昂昂溪区做核酸检测后，又把她劫往齐齐哈尔市富裕县看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，温雨飞被齐齐哈尔市建华区法院庭审。<span lang="EN-US">202012</span>月末被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">武桂琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">53</span>岁，黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员。哈尔滨市哈尔滨市依兰县公安局<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午对依兰县、佳木斯市桦川县两地法轮功学员实施绑架，到<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日共有<span lang="EN-US">29</span>人被绑架，其中十四名法轮功学员宋玉芝、施凤香、施凤兰、王云杰、周妍、邓术梅、宋孔华、武桂琴、卜宝玲、夏桂华、唐立飞、姚怀英、康艳玲、庞秀贤，与薛宏亮（未修炼法轮功）被长期关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭依兰县法院庭审。武桂琴被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">武桂芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">73</span>岁。黑龙江巴彦县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，黑龙江巴彦县龙泉乡派出所警察将七十三岁的武桂芝叫去派出所，然后，将其绑架到巴彦县公安局，由女警察轮班看守。后武桂芝被告知自己被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。 <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">武见男：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省籍人，基督徒，华西改革宗区会成员，四川省德阳市秋雨青草地归正教会长老，中国在押良心犯。因笃信基督，并在四川省德阳市秋雨青草地归正教会前长老郝鸣退休之后，由教会信众一致推举，被聘为该教会 新任职的长老级神职人员，故而在教会里有极好的口碑，但也成为中共四川当局需要严打狠批的重要对象；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日， 成都秋雨圣约教会突遭成都警方的大抓捕，王怡牧师夫妇及秋雨圣约教会的诸多神职人员，如覃德富、李英强、李子虎等长老、牧者和同工（即教会神职服侍人员）百余人尽被成都警方以涉嫌<span lang="EN-US">"</span>煽动颠覆国家政权罪<span lang="EN-US">"</span>或<span lang="EN-US">"</span>非法经营罪<span lang="EN-US">"</span>刑拘 ；后因打压扩大化，同年<span lang="EN-US">12 </span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-12</span>日，其所在四川省德阳市秋雨青草地归正教会亦受冲击，教会会所 被德阳市旌阳区警方与辖区城北街道办、小区等多方工作人员连手闯入，正在查经的信徒被驱离，教会正常的敬拜活动被 取缔，甚至提供教会租用房屋的房东也遭警方施压，被强行要求撕毁与教会签订的房屋租赁合同，让教会当天就得搬离会堂场所；因其与教会其他牧者、长老、同工与诸多信众拒绝了当局这一无理要求，表示仍将继续进入会堂敬拜 ，随其等神职人员之后频遭当局跟踪和监控，其教会也于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25 </span>日被四川省民政厅正式取缔<span lang="EN-US">;2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，因其曾与退休后又在成都市秋雨圣约教会供职的郝鸣长老、贵阳市仁爱教会的张春雷长老（现已被贵州当局抓捕）等人公开同情、支援已被抓捕判刑的王怡牧师，并勇于、乐于说明成都秋雨圣约 教会共度难关，随再遭当局更进一步强烈打压<span lang="EN-US">;</span>是日，其与其妻、郝鸣长老夫妇二人，以及教会的同工刘五一、刘永波、 蓝恩光等数人被四川省德阳市旌阳区警方统一抓走，两天之后，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其余人等都陆续被放，唯其及郝鸣长老被警方以涉嫌<span lang="EN-US">"</span>诈骗罪<span lang="EN-US">" </span>转为正式刑拘<span lang="EN-US">;2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24 </span>日，又被德阳市旌阳区检察院以同罪由正式批捕。目前被羁押于德阳市看守所（四川省德阳市双东镇龙凤村，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">618017</span>）信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/blog-post_80.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/blog-post_80.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">武全：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北律师武全<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日在新浪博客实名举报张家口市人大常委会副主任王志军。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，武全被张家口警方以涉嫌敲诈勒索罪刑事拘留。在对武全刑事拘留后，办案单位再向社会发出了线索征集的函件。此种先抓人再收集证据的知法犯法的行径在<span lang="EN-US">709</span>系列案中表现的淋漓尽致。这次又用在武全律师身上。令舆论哗然。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月获悉其遭张家口市桥西区法院重判<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吴碧林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，武汉市年过七旬法轮功学员。原是武汉市物资局的干部。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共迫害法轮功以来，吴碧林<span lang="EN-US">20</span>次被非法拘捕关押，平均每年一次，几乎每次都是在吴碧林被迫害致生命垂危时，相关机构怕承担责任，才将她放回。二零一一年吴碧林曾被江汉区法院判刑五年，由于身体原因监外执行。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，武汉市江岸区东立国际片警抓捕了吴碧林并非法抄家。六月初，汉阳区检察院批捕。吴碧林被关押在武汉市第一看守所（东西湖二支沟）。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被武汉市汉阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吴朝琪：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1992</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，广东省茂名市电白区人，广州打工人，自由信仰追求者，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。曾因<span lang="EN-US">16</span>岁时患有“肺中积水”，虽做手术，但几度复发，致其疾病未予治愈反使花费颇多；后因“肺中积水”再次复发，呼吸困难，随开始信仰并修炼法轮功，但自此开始屡受广东当局属下的“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”办公室严打迫害；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，曾因利用工余时间在广州市天河公园附近清理宣传栏中有关诬蔑、诽谤法轮功的内容，而被天河区天园派出所警方抓走，遭暴打，数次被脚踢、头撞墙等，之后被以涉嫌邪教罪刑拘，送广州市天河区看守所关押；同年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，又被转送到广东省法制教育学校接受洗脑式教育；因长期不被释放，其家人在为其聘请的两位维权律师帮助下逐级将控告信上告到广东省检察院、广东省公安厅等司法部门，终使其在被非法关押近<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月后得以取保获释；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，吴朝棋及其母亲林丽珍、其姨妈林燕梅三人先后突然被茂名市滨海新区、电白区及电城镇派出所警方等<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多人联合撬门抓走，后被以涉嫌邪教罪刑拘，羁押于茂名市第一看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，吴朝棋三人案被广东省茂名市茂南区法院统一在茂名市第一看守所内庭审；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，三人均被该法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”宣判；其中，吴朝棋被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元，其母亲林丽珍亦被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；其姨妈林燕梅被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千元；其不服上诉；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，经广东省茂名市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日；据悉，其在看守所时曾绝食抗议<span lang="EN-US">7</span>天，遭酷刑折磨，刚入狱时曾被匿名服刑。目前吴朝棋在广东省四会监狱（广东省肇庆市四会市济广塘监狱区，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">526237</span>）服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/5_19.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/5_19.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴春雄：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1986</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月出生，广东省揭阳市揭西县人，揭阳市榕城区东升街道办事处新河村建阳路南<span lang="EN-US">3</span>区居民，揭阳市创致科技有限公司负责人，自由信仰追求者，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月起，曾因信仰法轮功而从网上购置打印机、纸册、切纸机和装订机等工具，在其经营的创致科技有限公司及居民住宅区私印法轮功宣传手册，同时，又利用微信组建法轮功群，发布许多相关法轮功信息和图片等，随很快引起广东省揭阳市“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>办公室”注意，并对其等数人进行严密监控；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，因其公司的微信公众号出现有法轮功的宣传讯息，旋即被广东省揭阳市网员警觉，遂被揭阳市东升派出所警方从其所在公司抓走刑拘，其家及公司均遭查抄；另有其公司员工和友人唐建群、吴旭钦、陈晓彬、蔡林华等<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人亦被当天抓走，并被以涉嫌邪教罪刑拘；后被揭阳市榕城区检察院以“同案犯”、同罪名正式批捕，并被羁押于揭阳市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其<span lang="EN-US">1</span>行<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人案（另<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人被另案处理）被榕城区检察院正式起诉；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人案在广东省揭阳市榕城区法院统一受审；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，被该法院<span lang="EN-US">1</span>审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪” 枉法宣判；其中，<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">其被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">6</span>万元；</b>另有唐建群、吴旭钦、陈晓彬、蔡林华亦被分别判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月不等，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元—<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元不等；其等<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人不服判决，均向揭阳市中级法院提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，经广东省揭阳市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">吴春雄刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。</b>目前在广东省四会监狱（广东省肇庆市<span lang="EN-US">4</span>会市济广塘济广北路，广东省<span lang="EN-US">4</span>会监狱<span lang="EN-US">290</span>信箱，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">526237</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吴冬梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林农安县法轮功学员。女、<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">49</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，长春市农安县抓捕了<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多名法轮功学员。此次抓捕行动，是由长春市政法委和农安县政法委共同策划实施的。此次被抓捕的法轮功学员有</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张秀芝、高晓歧、蔡玉英、吴冬梅、于姣茹、单为和、赵秀兰、孙秀英、张敬元、孙凤仙、冯立齐、吕相富、董秀辉等<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">22</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">名法轮功学员被抓捕。他们被抓捕、构陷<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，有十几名法轮功学员被德惠市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>至<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。其中：吴冬梅</span>被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年；<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/5/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%9713%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%8C%E5%88%B0%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4-%E4%B8%AD%E6%B3%95%E7%BB%B4%E6%8C%81%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4-434381.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/5/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%9713%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%8C%E5%88%B0%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4-%E4%B8%AD%E6%B3%95%E7%BB%B4%E6%8C%81%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4-434381.html</span></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">吴淦：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1972</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出生，福建省福清市人，网名“屠夫”，退伍军人，知名维权围观者、人权捍卫者。近年来因频繁出现于诸多社会热点事件最前沿（如邓玉娇案、钱云会案、云南昆明小学生卖淫案、夏俊峰案等）而成为当局急于被维稳、打击的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年曾因为邓玉娇案和云南昆明小学生卖淫案网上维权， 而一跃成为网路知名维权围观者。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月曾因福州市晋安区政府对王庄地区进行征地强拆，其拟以杀猪宝典行为艺术进行维权声援，而被当地警方抓走训诫。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，因关注呼吁当局彻查披露庆安枪杀徐纯合真相，令当局十分恼火，而对其实施威胁，迫使其被迫逃离北京。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，又因声援江西乐平死刑冤案，并以“卖身筹款”的行为艺术举牌帮助律师在江西高院门前争取律师阅卷权，而被江西省南昌市警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被福建警方以涉“寻衅滋事罪”、“诽谤罪”刑拘，同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被厦门市检察院以涉“寻衅滋事罪”和“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日获悉，其案件已被转交天津警方处理。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日其案被天津巿第二中级法院秘密开庭受审，至<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日终被该法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，剥权<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。羁押期间，曾累受酷刑折磨，甚至被强迫去住院进行“虐待式治疗”，为此，其不得不通过律师发出个人四不声明，以表明自己绝不自杀、不接受官方指定律师、不认罪和不上官媒悔罪的决心。目前被羁押于天津市第二看守所<span lang="EN-US">D101</span>室。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴刚：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1956</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日出生，天津市和平区人，天津市某中学教师，抗强拆维权公民，中国在押维权人士。早期吴刚曾因其住宅被天津地方政府强拆，后其工作岗位又遭辞退，随被迫走上维权上访之路；近年来，曾因参与多起维权活动，尤其是参与声援天津北辰抗暴维权者王国廷案被当局枉法重判、维权公民在天津市人大门前举牌进行和平请愿等，而遭当局多次拘捕打压：<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日吴刚曾被天津警方以涉嫌“扰乱公共场所秩序罪”行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月又被警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日再次被警方以涉嫌“扰乱单位秩序罪”行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，吴刚再次因参与维权抗争而被天津市和平区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被以同罪名转正式逮捕，关押在天津市南开区看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，吴刚案件在天津市和平区法院开庭受审；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被天津市中级法院第两次庭审，终以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，吴刚刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，因吴刚一直要求约见区人大代表，遂于<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月中旬突然失踪；<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，知其被天津市河西区大营门派出所警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘。目前被羁押于天津市河西区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/blog-post_75.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/blog-post_75.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴俊萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省保定市独居老人、法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1949</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被警察入室抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被保定市高阳县法院庭审；<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日法院通知家属，吴俊萍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吴葛健雄：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南省长沙市人，外称“小吴”，弱势群体维权诉讼代理人，民间公益组织“长沙富能”<span lang="EN-US">NGO</span>成员，中国在押政治犯。因积极从事公益维权活动，代理多起维权诉讼案件等，深受大众欢迎；近年来因在参与公益维权同时，与机构其他<span lang="EN-US">CEO</span>成员和海外人道服务机构往来较多，随遭中共当局警觉及严密监控；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，因对香港「反送中」抗议有同情言论，<span lang="EN-US"> 7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日随与另两位公益成员一同被湖南省长沙市国家安全局警方从公司办公室带走，且被旋即以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘；其父已收到他的拘留通知书；据悉，其事先委托代理律师向长沙市国家安全局了解详情遭拒，仅告知被控涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”，原因不明，疑与香港正在进行的反送中风潮有关；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被长沙市国家安全局以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”转正式逮捕。后遭强迫辞退自己做律师的父亲代理，当局强行派官派律师，目前已经进入司法审判阶段并且已经开庭审理，可家人对案情却一无所知。目前被羁押于湖南省国家安全厅看守所。长沙富能发起人程渊的妻子施明磊综合各渠道信息，获悉长沙公益仨程渊、吴葛健雄、刘大志三人已在北京时间<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午被长沙市中级法院判决，吴葛健雄被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刘大志被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，程渊刑期<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。吴葛健雄<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月被转去赤山监狱服刑，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_98.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_98.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴玲娥：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西省临汾金灯台家庭教会同工、基督徒。山西临汾金灯堂教案受害者之一。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，山西临汾金灯堂教会九位负责人和同工被警方抓捕，其中包括曾为信仰坐牢<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年的王晓光牧师和他的妻子、曾为信仰坐牢<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年的杨荣丽姊妹。后来一些同工被取保候审，又有一些新的人被抓捕。现在还在看守所的有<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人<span lang="EN-US">: </span>王晓光牧师及妻子杨荣丽，李双平、董勇勇、赵国爱、霍壮平、吴玲娥。这七人于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被移送检察院审查起诉。据悉，批捕和移送检察院审查起诉的罪名都是涉嫌“诈骗罪”。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_39.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_39.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴美芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东清远的失地农民维权代表。其所在的连州市丰阳镇其美村因为修高速公路需要征地，原村里负责人于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年趁村民外出做事，冒充村民在征地协议上签字，并侵吞集体土地征收补偿款。正在外面打工的其丈夫郭雪来接村民电话，立即回家和村民一起到镇政府讨说法，结果刚到镇政府大门口，十几村民就被抓捕了，其中郭雪来被以“扰乱国家工作机关秩序罪”判刑三年！后吴美芬为了替夫伸冤而被迫上访。郭雪来说：去年八月份我爱人在北京信访时，给我们地方政府接访的人骗回来，说要保护我们的合法权益，解决我们的合理诉求，一个月后我收到逮捕通知书，说她“涉嫌扰乱国家机关工作秩序罪”关押在铅山县看守所，就是这样得到党和政府的“保护”。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初，郭雪来接到连州市法院电话，问要不要给他涉嫌“扰乱国家机关工作秩序罪”的妻子吴美芬安排援助律师，郭雪来很清楚，所谓援助律师实际上就是官派律师，纯属为公检法“点炮”的，就断然拒绝了。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吴文章：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">秦皇岛市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，秦皇岛市山海关公安分局在左洪涛、崔秋荣夫妇开的“佳合中介”抓捕了夫妻二人及吴文章、杨晓勇、袁素静及李国爱等五名法轮功学员，抄查中野蛮地抢劫了中介周转资金十余万元现金及电动车一辆和其它办公用品。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，对吴文章、左洪涛、崔秋荣等人以莫须有的罪名批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，昌黎县法院对四名法轮功学员左洪涛、刘长富、吴文章、李国爱与左洪涛的妻子崔秋荣（不炼功）五人开庭。后判处左洪涛<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年有期徒刑，吴文章<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，李国爱<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刘长富<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，左洪涛妻子崔秋荣（没炼功）<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年零几个月（已获释）。吴文章刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">吴向洋：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1980</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年代后期出生，广西贵港市平南县人，网络工程师，网络<span lang="EN-US">VPN</span>服务器搭建者，境外网站登陆软件服务商。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2010</span>年曾就读于中国人民大学，毕业后曾任职于腾讯科技（深圳）有限公司，辞职后自创企业“深圳千里通联科技公司”。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2017</span>年，因在网上自己搭建<span lang="EN-US">VPN</span>服务器并提供会员账号和登录软件，以供登录后可浏览境外网站，并将一些<span lang="EN-US">VPN</span>会员账号密码写到硬件路由器上<span lang="EN-US">,</span>使得修改过的路由器能够直接登录<span lang="EN-US">VPN</span>，以更好地实现可收听境外网站音<span lang="EN-US">/</span>视频节目的功能，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年被中国当局网警获悉，同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>、<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份被贵港市平南县警方刑拘。后被贵港市平南县检察院以涉嫌“非法经营罪”正式逮捕，控其在未取得《增值电信业务经营许可证》的情况下<span lang="EN-US">,</span>在网络上销售了<span lang="EN-US">VPN</span>代理服务<span lang="EN-US">,</span>同时还利用“淘宝网”以开设网店和在互联网开设“凡狗<span lang="EN-US">VPN</span>”网站等方式，向一般用户出租或销售<span lang="EN-US">VPN</span>软件、<span lang="EN-US">VPN</span>路由器硬件<span lang="EN-US">,</span>交易数千次<span lang="EN-US">,</span>非法经营额达<span lang="EN-US">792638</span>元<span lang="EN-US">,</span>非法获利约<span lang="EN-US">50</span>元，所以“根据《中华人民共和国电信条例》和《中国人民共和国刑法》等相关法律规定<span lang="EN-US">,</span>涉嫌非法经营罪”。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月其被广西贵港市平南县法院一审以“非法经营罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。目前被羁押于广西平南县看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴秀琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省白山市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">53</span>岁，家住吉林省白山市靖宇县。在中共对法轮功的疯狂迫害中，吴秀琴多次被抓捕、关押，在看守所、劳教所、监狱多次遭受酷刑。<span lang="EN-US"> 2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日下午，靖宇县公安局国保大队大队长于学军，闯入吴秀琴租住的公寓，实施抓捕、抄家、抢劫，并把她关押到白山市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日吴秀琴被白山市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/6/%E5%B1%A1%E9%81%AD%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3-%E5%90%89%E6%9E%97%E7%99%BD%E5%B1%B1%E5%B8%82%E5%90%B4%E7%A7%80%E7%90%B4%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-434439.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/6/%E5%B1%A1%E9%81%AD%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3-%E5%90%89%E6%9E%97%E7%99%BD%E5%B1%B1%E5%B8%82%E5%90%B4%E7%A7%80%E7%90%B4%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-434439.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吴旭钦：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东揭阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，广东揭阳市揭西县法轮功学员吴春雄在揭阳榕城区新河村自己的公司被揭阳市公安局东升派出所抓捕，公司的几名员工吴旭钦等也被抓捕。据悉，是公司的微信公众号出现有法轮功的真相。随后，派出所人员胁迫吴旭钦带他们到家里非法抄家，并抓捕了吴旭钦的母亲陈晓彬，还用封条把家门都封了。吴春雄原本生意很好的公司全面停运，同时很多私人物品被非法抄走。吴春雄、吴旭钦、陈晓彬、蔡林华等被关押在看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月上旬，广东揭阳市榕城区法院在揭阳市判法轮功学员吴旭钦<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吴艳华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江省大庆市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日吴艳华与丈夫关兴涛被抓捕、构陷，后被大庆市让胡路区法院冤判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，现在被关押在黑龙江省女子监狱遭受迫害。其丈夫关兴涛被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。吴艳华刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/2/26/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-421367.html#2122522533-1"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/2/26/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-421367.html#2122522533-1</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴玉喜：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北鄂州维权人士，湖北省鄂州市梁湖区太和镇花黄村上吴湾村民，因政府侵占其耕地和宅基地、剥夺其被救济权而上访，因上访吴玉喜长期被地方当局非法监控维稳。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，吴玉喜被地方官员从北京带回来后强制隔离了一次；<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日辖区警察又上门要强行带她去隔离，在她坚持拒绝下没被带走。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日从北京带回后即被隔离关押的湖北鄂州维权人士吴玉喜的家属收到逮捕通知书。遂获悉，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，吴玉喜被梁子湖区检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”批准逮捕，现羁押在鄂州市公安局第一看守所。地址：鄂州市鄂城区葛山大道<span lang="EN-US">46</span>号。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_49.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_49.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">吴泽衡：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1967</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日出生，广东省揭阳市惠来县人，佛教徒，“华藏宗门”创始人，人称“行武禅师”，原“国际生命科学研究中心”香港总干事、亚洲部执行主席。自幼信仰佛教，<span lang="EN-US">1978</span>年起潜心学习并武术、兵法、医道等多元知识，后在少林寺拜高僧释德禅大和尚为师，研读经书，<span lang="EN-US">19</span>岁已成为少林寺史上最年轻的总监坛；<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年自创气功门派“华藏功”，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年更名为“华藏宗门”；<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年已在海内外颇具声望；<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日曾撰文并上书《和谐社会的具体建议》，建议中共当局政治透明及对政治体制改革，因涉及信仰、党外监督、有限政府、选举等问题而被当局严控，后被刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被北京警方正式逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被北京市高级法院以“非法经营罪”、“擅自发行股票罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，并惨遭狱中酷刑虐待；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月获释后，其恪守信仰理念，再次发声坚称自己“对中华民族忠贞不渝，扶持正法，维护社会和谐统一”，且力推开展大型慈善活动，发起“辟谷行善、日行一善”，“公民互爱运动”等活动；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日曾因国际宗教自由委员会认定其为<span lang="EN-US">88</span>世佛教直系传人，并接到多个国际宗教组织的访问邀请，而被当局拒发出境旅游签证；随着中共当局近年来对宗教打压迫害程度的加强，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日其再次因政治及宗教信仰因素被珠海市警方以涉“利用邪教破坏法律实施罪”刑拘，其住地被查抄；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日其被以涉“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”、强奸罪、诈骗罪和“生产、销售有毒、有害食品罪”四罪名提起公诉；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被广东省珠海市中级法院以上述四罪名判处无期徒刑，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">715</span>万元，其宗教派别被定为邪教组织，二审后依然维持原判。目前其已从广东省四会监狱转送至新疆某监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吴志群：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1949</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年生，重庆市合川东津沱重棉四厂退休工人、法轮功学员。吴志群因发放法轮功<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘，被不明真相的人恶意举报，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被国保绑架。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">乌木别提•卡斯木（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市巴里巴盖乡人，哈萨克族，穆斯林。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">乌木别提﹒卡斯木<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁</b>，阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，纳杂尔﹒叶尔江<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，沙部旦﹒沙伊合约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，耶尔肯别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，肯杰别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，因他们分别在私下里进行了穆斯林传统常规祷告仪式，而被中共新疆伊犁市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰当局知晓后拘捕，遂很快被阿尔泰市地方法院以“非法从事宗教活动”和“从事宗教极端活动”为由分别判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年不等刑期。目前各人具体判刑不详，刑至日期不详，服刑监狱不详，服刑状况及健康程度等不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><a name="_Hlk52050620"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></a></p>
